Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Springfield, MO, February 7, 2024</b><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> &#8211; </font>O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;O&#8217;Reilly&#8221;) (<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Nasdaq: &#160;</font>ORLY), a leading retailer in the automotive aftermarket industry, today announced record revenue and earnings for its fourth quarter and full-year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023. &#160;The results represent 31 consecutive years of comparable store sales growth and record revenue and operating income for O&#8217;Reilly since becoming a public company in April of 1993.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">4</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">th</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Brad Beckham, O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;), commented, &#8220;We are pleased to report another solid quarter, highlighted by a comparable store sales increase of 3.4%, on top of the very strong 9.0% comparable store sales increase Team O&#8217;Reilly delivered in the fourth quarter last year. &#160;Our Team once again generated double-digit professional comparable store sales growth, while also successfully navigating the anticipated year-over-year pressure we experienced on the DIY side of our business, resulting from the extremely strong, weather-driven sales we produced in the fourth quarter of 2022. &#160;In total, our comparable store sales performance exceeded our expectations for the quarter, driven by Team O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s relentless focus on providing the highest levels of service in the industry. &#160;We would like to express our appreciation to each of our over 90,000 Team Members for their unwavering commitment to going above and beyond for our customers each and every day.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased $188 million, or 5%, to $3.83 billion from $3.64 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the fourth quarter increased 6% to $1.97 billion (or 51.3% of sales) from $1.85 billion (or 50.9% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Selling, general and administrative expenses (&#8220;SG&amp;A&#8221;) for the fourth quarter increased 7% to $1.25 billion (or 32.6% of sales) from $1.17 billion (or 32.2% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for the fourth quarter increased 5% to $719 million (or 18.8% of sales) from $682 million (or 18.7% of sales) for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased $24 million, or 5%, to $553 million (or 14.4% of sales) from $529 million (or 14.5% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the fourth quarter increased 11% to $9.26 on 60 million shares versus $8.37 on 63 million shares for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Full-Year Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Beckham continued, &#8220;We delivered another year of exceptional, profitable growth, highlighted by a 7.9% increase in comparable store sales and a full-year diluted earnings per share increase of 15% to $38.47. &#160;I would like to congratulate our entire Team for their 31st<sup style="font-size:8.25pt;vertical-align:top;"> </sup>consecutive year of annual comparable store sales growth and record earnings. &#160;2023 was also a very successful expansion year for our Company, with the successful opening of 186 new stores, the growth of our store and distribution footprint into Puerto Rico, and the opening of a large, modern distribution center in Guadalajara, Mexico.&#8221;</p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr style="background-color:#000000;clear:both;color:#000000;height:2pt;line-height:0;margin-bottom:30pt;margin-left:5.88%;margin-right:5.88%;margin-top:30pt;page-break-after:always;width:88.24%;border-width:0;"><div style="max-width:100%;padding-left:5.88%;padding-right:5.88%;position:relative;"><div style="clear:both;max-width:100%;position:relative;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased $1.40 billion, or 10%, to $15.81 billion from $14.41 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased 10% to $8.10 billion (or 51.3% of sales) from $7.38 billion (or 51.2% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;SG&amp;A for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased 11% to $4.92 billion (or 31.1% of sales) from $4.43 billion (or 30.7% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased 8% to $3.19 billion (or 20.2% of sales) from $2.95 billion (or 20.5% of sales) for the same period one year ago.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased $174 million, or 8%, to $2.35 billion (or 14.8% of sales) from $2.17 billion (or 15.1% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, increased 15% to $38.47 on 61 million shares versus $33.44 on 65 million shares for the same period one year ago.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Beckham concluded, &#8220;Our success in 2023 is a testament to our Team&#8217;s hard work, and as we look forward to 2024, we remain absolutely confident in our Team&#8217;s ability to consistently execute our dual market strategy and provide the best customer service in the industry. &#160;Our Team has repeatedly proven their ability to aggressively gain market share and profitably grow our business, and we are extremely excited to welcome our new Canadian Team Members to the O&#8217;Reilly family, with the closing of the Groupe Del Vasto acquisition in January. &#160;O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s experienced leadership is already working closely with our seasoned management team in Canada, and we look forward to capitalizing on the long-term profitable growth opportunities in our new markets as we extend our track record of profitable growth throughout North America.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">4</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">th</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter and Full-Year Comparable Store Sales Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Comparable store sales are calculated based on the change in sales for U.S. stores open at least one year and exclude sales of specialty machinery, sales to independent parts stores, and sales to Team Members. &#160;Online sales for ship-to-home orders and pick-up-in-store orders for U.S. stores open at least one year are included in the comparable store sales calculation. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 3.4% for the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, on top of 9.0% for the same period one year ago. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 7.9% for the year ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, on top of 6.4% for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Share Repurchase Program</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">During the fourth quarter ended December&#160;31,&#160;2023, the Company repurchased 0.6 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $922.86, for a total investment of $560 million. &#160;During the year ended December 31, 2023, the Company repurchased 3.6 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $883.13, for a total investment of $3.15 billion. &#160;Excise tax on shares repurchased, assessed at one percent of the fair market value of net shares repurchased, was $28.8 million for the year ended December 31, 2023. &#160;Subsequent to the end of the fourth quarter and through the date of this release, the Company repurchased an additional 0.1 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $967.63, for a total investment of $102 million. &#160;The Company has repurchased a total of 94.2 million shares of its common stock under its share repurchase program since the inception of the program in January of 2011 and through the date of this release, at an average price of $247.16, for a total aggregate investment of $23.28 billion. &#160;As of the date of this release, the Company had approximately $2.47 billion remaining under its current share repurchase authorizations. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr style="background-color:#000000;clear:both;color:#000000;height:2pt;line-height:0;margin-bottom:30pt;margin-left:5.88%;margin-right:5.88%;margin-top:30pt;page-break-after:always;width:88.24%;border-width:0;"><div generally accepted accounting principles (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;). &#160;These items include adjusted debt to earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, amortization, share-based compensation, and rent (&#8220;EBITDAR&#8221;) and free cash flow. &#160;The Company does not, nor does it suggest investors should, consider such non-GAAP financial measures in isolation from, or as a substitute for, GAAP financial information. &#160;The Company believes that the presentation of adjusted debt to EBITDAR and free cash flow provide meaningful supplemental information to both management and investors that is indicative of the Company&#8217;s core operations. &#160;The Company has included a reconciliation of this additional information to the most comparable GAAP measure in the table above and the selected financial information below. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Completion of Leadership Succession Plan</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">O&#8217;Reilly completed its previously announced Leadership Succession Plan on January 31, 2024, with the retirement of O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s CEO Greg Johnson, and the simultaneous promotions of Brad Beckham to the role of CEO and Brent Kirby to the role of President. &#160;In addition, on February 1, 2024, the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) nominated Greg Johnson to serve on O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s Board, to be voted upon by the Company&#8217;s shareholders at O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s Annual Shareholders&#8217; Meeting, which will be held in May of 2024. &#160;Mr. Johnson is being nominated to replace the Board seat currently held by Jay Burchfield, who is expected to retire from the Board at the end of his current director term in May, consistent with the Board&#8217;s mandatory retirement age policy.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New express our sincere appreciation to Greg for his 41 years of dedicated service to O&#8217;Reilly, as well as reiterate our confidence in the Company&#8217;s future under the leadership of Brad and Brent, who are both very well respected and proven leaders with O&#8217;Reilly. &#160;I would also like to take this opportunity to thank Jay Burchfield for his guidance as the Company&#8217;s Lead Director and congratulate him on his upcoming Board retirement. &#160;Finally, I would like to relay our excitement with Greg Johnson&#8217;s </p></div><div Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">About O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. was founded in 1957 by the O&#8217;Reilly family and is one of the largest specialty retailers of automotive aftermarket parts, tools, supplies, equipment, and accessories in the United States, serving both the do-it-yourself and professional service provider markets. &#160;Visit the Company&#8217;s website at <u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">www.OReillyAuto.com</u> for additional information about O&#8217;Reilly, including access to online shopping and current promotions, store locations, hours and services, employment opportunities, and other programs. &#160;As of December&#160;31,&#160;2023, the Company operated 6,157 stores across 48 U.S. states, Puerto Rico, and Mexico. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New
